<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_21a767db-a464-4b99-ad38-397ef954fa08'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer7457893184611973901">It's Nantucket wedding season, also known as summer-the sight of a bride racing down Main Street is as common as the sun setting at Madaket Beach. The Otis-Winbury wedding promises to be an event to remember: the groom's wealthy parents have spared no expense to host a lavish ceremony at their oceanfront estate.<br/><br/>But it's going to be memorable for all the wrong reasons after</span>
  <span id="freeText7457893184611973901" style="display:none">It's Nantucket wedding season, also known as summer-the sight of a bride racing down Main Street is as common as the sun setting at Madaket Beach. The Otis-Winbury wedding promises to be an event to remember: the groom's wealthy parents have spared no expense to host a lavish ceremony at their oceanfront estate.<br /><br />But it's going to be memorable for all the wrong reasons after tragedy strikes: a body is discovered in Nantucket Harbor just hours before the ceremony-and everyone in the wedding party is suddenly a suspect. As Chief of Police Ed Kapenash interviews the bride, the groom, the groom's famous mystery-novelist mother, and even a member of his own family, he discovers that every wedding is a minefield-and no couple is perfect. Featuring beloved characters from The Castaways, Beautiful Day, and A Summer Affair, The Perfect Couple proves once again that Elin Hilderbrand is the queen of the summer beach read.</span>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I think the author purposely did not tell us the answer to that -- and to a couple of other things "we" were unsure about. Although we would like to h<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I think the author purposely did not tell us the answer to that -- and to a couple of other things "we" were unsure about. Although we would like to have everything neatly tied up -- I think it leaves us to continue thinking about the book long after we finish it. I told my husband that I had just finished a good book -- and he wanted to hear about it. There were so many different characters with such different lives that it was hard to put it into a few bullet points. Certainly the author left me hungry for more -- now I want to read all her other books and see if they are as good.<br /><a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

<div id="review_2404733124" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2404733124" />
    <a title="Melissa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9684061-melissa"><img alt="Melissa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528750408p2/9684061.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2404733124?book_show_action=true">May 27, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa" href="/user/show/9684061-melissa">Melissa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/39293747-the-perfect-couple">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9684061-melissa?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9684061-melissa?shelf=must-read-again">must-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9684061-melissa?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9684061-melissa?shelf=best-of-the-best">best-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9684061-melissa?shelf=unforgettable-reads">unforgettable-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9684061-melissa?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9684061-melissa?shelf=womens-fiction">womens-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2404733124" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1252189681489741019">I hate to play favorites, but in this case, <i>I don't feel like I have a choice.</i> In my humble opinion, this is <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/88301.Elin_Hilderbrand' title='Elin Hilderbrand' rel='nofollow noopener'>Elin Hilderbrand</a>'s best work yet. Combining her signature backdrop, riveting cast of characters and penchant for teasing the craveable local fare <b>
  <i>with</i>
</b> the suspense of a murder mystery—you better believe, I soaked up every moment in the Nantucket sun. <br/> <br/>This year, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/88301.Elin_Hilderbrand' title='Elin Hilderbrand' rel='nofollow noopener'>Elin Hilderbrand</a> lures readers back to the picturesque Nantucket island with the invitation to a prominent wedding. Until th</span>
  <span id="freeText1252189681489741019" style="display:none">I hate to play favorites, but in this case, <i>I don't feel like I have a choice.</i> In my humble opinion, this is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/88301.Elin_Hilderbrand" title="Elin Hilderbrand" rel="nofollow noopener">Elin Hilderbrand</a>'s best work yet. Combining her signature backdrop, riveting cast of characters and penchant for teasing the craveable local fare <b>
  <i>with</i>
</b> the suspense of a murder mystery—you better believe, I soaked up every moment in the Nantucket sun. <br /> <br />This year, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/88301.Elin_Hilderbrand" title="Elin Hilderbrand" rel="nofollow noopener">Elin Hilderbrand</a> lures readers back to the picturesque Nantucket island with the invitation to a prominent wedding. Until the morning of, Benji and Celeste’s nuptials are poised to be the event of the summer. Loving couple, coveted wedding planner and a mother-in-law ensuring every minute detail is just so—<i>what could possibly go wrong</i>? Turns out, something far worse than anyone could fathom—let alone the bride. <br /><br />Celeste wakes on the morning of her special day to find her only friend and maid of honor, Merritt, floating along the shore of her in-law’s stunning Summerland compound. The question becomes, was it an untimely accident or something far more sinister? <br /><br />Through the investigative work of Chief Ed Kapenash (<i>you may remember him from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6080822.The_Castaways" title="The Castaways by Elin Hilderbrand" rel="nofollow noopener">The Castaways</a></i>), an unraveling of the many alibis and a host of memories from multiple perspectives, Elin takes us back to the beginning—to how Benji and Celeste came to be <i>the perfect couple</i> set to say “<i>I do</i>”. In doing so, Hilderbrand incites a frenzy, holding the reader captive as one tightly-held secret after another is revealed. Reminiscent of the game of Clue, <i>everyone</i> takes their turn at playing the suspect. <br /><br />There’s something to be said about Hilderbrand’s ability to pen such distinct and compelling characters. You may not love them all for who they are or condone the situations they get themselves into, but there’s no denying, you want to stick around to hear what they have to say. <br /><br />For me, it was the bride Celeste that stole the show. A breath of fresh air—by Nantucket and leading lady standards—unassuming and uninterested in trying to impress people, she’s distinctly Celeste. A zoologist driven by her love of nature, she’s a true friend, loving daughter and a woman caught up in the whirlwind of her first ever relationship. Her journey just might make you ponder, does each bad deed committed, in turn, set something else in motion?<br /><br />There is a HUGE piece of the plot that I want to gush about to NO END. But I won’t for the sake of ruining it for someone else. What I will say, because I have to say <i>something</i>, there’s an enviable level of wanting and intense longing that completely stole my heart. I found myself turning the pages with bated breath in anticipation of what was to come for these <i>two</i>. My one hope—somehow, some way—we’ll cross paths with this couple again. Maybe in a future book?<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Yes, but none of those flowers are from me. I want you to look at this bouqet and know just how besotted I am with you.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br /><i>*Thank you to Little, Brown and Company for providing my copy.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1252189681489741019" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2389114018" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13840064518563060865">Ahhhhh Nantucket in the summer is bliss! It is a lovely place to vacation. It also serves as the perfect place for a wedding, the beach and a murder! <br/><br/>The Otis-Winbury is going to be one to remember! The groom's family has arranged for the wedding to be the event of the season. A wedding that people will be talking about for years to come! And it will be remembered but not for the reasons they want it to be. In the early morning hours on the day of the wedding, the maid of honor is found dead. Ch</span>
  <span id="freeText13840064518563060865" style="display:none">Ahhhhh Nantucket in the summer is bliss! It is a lovely place to vacation. It also serves as the perfect place for a wedding, the beach and a murder! <br /><br />The Otis-Winbury is going to be one to remember! The groom's family has arranged for the wedding to be the event of the season. A wedding that people will be talking about for years to come! And it will be remembered but not for the reasons they want it to be. In the early morning hours on the day of the wedding, the maid of honor is found dead. Chief of Police Ed Kapenash is leading the investigation and everyone in the wedding party is a suspect.<br /><br />The story unfolds through various character's perspectives and timelines. It becomes clear that almost everyone in this book has a secret - BIG scandalous secrets. But just because one has a secret doesn't make them guilty of murder, or does it?<br /><br />This may be the quintessential beach read of summer 2018. There are secrets, family secrets, lies, deceptions, suspense and mystery. This was a very fast read that had me guessing along with Chief Kapenash as to the identity of the “murderer" . This book is pure enjoyment. As the investigation unfolds and the stories and backstories are told, the reader may suspect several characters of murder in this whodunnit. This book doesn't involve a lot of thinking, again, it's pure entertainment which makes it perfect for a summer/beach/poolside read. Another plus is that there is nothing graphic in this book, which means most readers will be able to read and enjoy this book!<br /><br />Thank you to NetGalley and Little, Brown and Company who provided me with a copy of this book in exchange for an honest review. The opinions in this review are my own.<br /><br />Read more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.openbookpost.com">www.openbookpost.com</a><br /></span>

<div id="review_2429961185" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2429961185" />
    <a title="Skyler Autumn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12859342-skyler-autumn"><img alt="Skyler Autumn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1534857879p2/12859342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2429961185?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Skyler Autumn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Skyler Autumn" href="/user/show/12859342-skyler-autumn">Skyler Autumn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2429961185" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13303194632960852328"><b> 2 Stars </b> <br/><br/>Slated as this years must have summer beach read I went into this novel not expecting to be intellectually stimulated. Obviously this was going to be light and easy read, but there's nothing wrong with switching off your brain and delving into something easy, breezy (mentally trying to stop myself from saying cover girl but I can't) if at least it's fun. This novel was fun for the first 30% then it got boring, and then it got long and when I finally hit the last chapter it took that tu</span>
  <span id="freeText13303194632960852328" style="display:none"><b> 2 Stars </b> <br /><br />Slated as this years must have summer beach read I went into this novel not expecting to be intellectually stimulated. Obviously this was going to be light and easy read, but there's nothing wrong with switching off your brain and delving into something easy, breezy (mentally trying to stop myself from saying cover girl but I can't) if at least it's fun. This novel was fun for the first 30% then it got boring, and then it got long and when I finally hit the last chapter it took that turn to just plain irritating. <br /><br />The Perfect Couple is centred around Benji and Celeste's fairytale wedding on Nantucket... spoiler alert the wedding isn't as fairytale as you're led to believe. I know, shocker! When the Maid of Honour Merritt is found floating around the ocean dead, on the day of the supposed dream wedding, everything is flipped on its head as readers are taken into the secret lives of the many guests. <br /><br />The concept although sounding like a fun murder mystery on the island took on a stereotypical chick-lit format about half way through making me feel as if this book had tricked me. What was slated as a murder mystery/whodunnit soon became a wish washy jumble of chapters about different romances of the many attendees of the wedding. The ending especially had me freakin pissed. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I'm sorry you are going to have a murder investigation for one whole day you can't figure it out that very second so you might as well rule it an accident? What kind of small town hillbilly cops are these, after an exhaustive investigation for 24 hours we got bored, tired and hungry decided to rule it a suicide because it's dinner time and I can't be missing that. It just made it all the more infuriating because it was then when I knew the authors mystery ploy was just bullshit. She wrote a chick-lit book and tried to disguise it as a mystery. Own your chick-litness from the start just don't false advertise me lady!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I also found myself being increasingly frustrated with how women were being portrayed in this novel. For a female author she really enjoyed painting women as sluts, bitches or virginal. Women were either prizes of male affection or shameful flirts that lured men into cheating the one dimensional brush this female author chose to paint the women in her novel was disheartening to say the least. <br /><br />And don't get me started on the central romance! That love at first sight stick, I will betray everyone I love for this random woman/man I've spent a day with is such nonsense that I can't even wrap my mind around it in my novels. I have an easier time believing in the possibility that there is a Hogwarts somewhere out there then freakin love at first sight. It was a patronizing and unrealistic love where the male in question would say belittling things like you're just so real compared to the women I know. What the fuck does that mean? If a guy told me I'm not like other girls or I'm real compared to other women. I'd tell him I don't need him to put down my entire gender to give me a patronizing compliment. This novel basically can be summed up by the fact men are the worst and women are prizes to be won and then disposed of when the man is done with them. There you go! I summed the novel up for you, now you don't have to read it. Your Welcome.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13303194632960852328" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8046541721996668206"><b> 4 stars for this tantalizing, indulgent mystery that was so much more addictive than watching a reality show or soap opera! </b> <br/><br/>The Perfect Couple is set in Nantucket, amidst the no expense spared paradise of sand, sun, beautiful wealthy people, privilege, secrets, lies and of course murder.   <span id="freeText8046541721996668206" style="display:none"><b> 4 stars for this tantalizing, indulgent mystery that was so much more addictive than watching a reality show or soap opera! </b> <br /><br />The Perfect Couple is set in Nantucket, amidst the no expense spared paradise of sand, sun, beautiful wealthy people, privilege, secrets, lies and of course murder. To say I could not resist this book would be an understatement. I literally had to force myself to put it down and I eagerly picked it up any chance I got. <br /><br />Benji and Celeste are set to be married until the bride finds her best friend and maid-of-honor, Merritt's body floating in the water. What follows is the unraveling of so much juicy deceit and so many secrets that you will not be able to turn the pages fast enough. With so many characters and so many secrets you can't help but suspect everyone! Hilderbrand did an amazing job unfolding this whodunnit. I will admit that I had suspicions about what happened but I did not have all the logistics worked out. I was very satisfied with the ending and pleased that I did not have it all figured out. <br /><br /><b>This is by far my favorite Hilderbrand to date and one that will be difficult for her to beat in my mind!</b></span>

<div id="review_2882244531" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Brandice" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36348070-brandice"><img alt="Brandice" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1582594594p2/36348070.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2882244531" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16413240488079416792">I couldn’t get enough of <i>The Perfect Couple</i>, a quintessential summer read, which I absorbed in the perfect setting at a lakehouse this extended holiday weekend. <br/><br/>Benji and Celeste are scheduled to get married at Benji’s family estate in Nantucket on Saturday but tragedy strikes the morning of the wedding when the maid of honor is found dead on the property. Nantucket Police Chief, Ed, and a handsome detective, Nick, are called to the scene to find out what happened and assess if there was foul pl</span>
  <span id="freeText16413240488079416792" style="display:none">I couldn’t get enough of <i>The Perfect Couple</i>, a quintessential summer read, which I absorbed in the perfect setting at a lakehouse this extended holiday weekend. <br /><br />Benji and Celeste are scheduled to get married at Benji’s family estate in Nantucket on Saturday but tragedy strikes the morning of the wedding when the maid of honor is found dead on the property. Nantucket Police Chief, Ed, and a handsome detective, Nick, are called to the scene to find out what happened and assess if there was foul play or if her death was an accident. <br /><br />Even with glitz, glam, and wealth in Nantucket, <b><i>everyone</i> has secrets</b>, which are revealed to Nick and Ed as they interview various members of the wedding party, families, and other guests. Along with the current investigation, the story flashes back in time, showing how Celeste and Benji met as well as the role of other characters including Benji’s parents, Tag and Greer, the best man, Shooter, the maid of honor, Merritt, and Celeste’s parents, Karen and Bruce. Some characters were likable while others definitely weren’t, and many weren’t who they initially seemed to be. <br /><br />I was hooked on <i>The Perfect Couple</i> from the get-go! Given death is involved, there are some sad elements in the book, including another storyline I wasn’t expecting, but these did not detract from my thorough enjoyment in reading it. The mystery of Merritt’s death had me guessing until the end, and I was satisfied with the story’s conclusion. I’ve been a Hilderbrand fan for a few years now - She writes about people so <i>well</i>. I have to say, <i>The Perfect Couple</i> is my favorite of her books. Highly recommend for a captivating summer read!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16413240488079416792" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5398636629590785193"><b>4 perfect beach read stars to The Perfect Couple!</b> 🏝 🏝 🏝 🏝 <br/><br/>I discovered Elin Hilderbrand a couple years ago, well after she was proclaimed the queen of beach reads. While her books may be “beachy” (i.e., set on Nantucket), they are well-written and full of depth. The Perfect Couple is Hilderbrand’s first foray into murder mystery writing and also incorporates some beloved characters from her past books.<br/><br/>Wedding season is synonymous for “summer people” on Nantucket, and that is when the island is u</span>
  <span id="freeText5398636629590785193" style="display:none"><b>4 perfect beach read stars to The Perfect Couple!</b> 🏝 🏝 🏝 🏝 <br /><br />I discovered Elin Hilderbrand a couple years ago, well after she was proclaimed the queen of beach reads. While her books may be “beachy” (i.e., set on Nantucket), they are well-written and full of depth. The Perfect Couple is Hilderbrand’s first foray into murder mystery writing and also incorporates some beloved characters from her past books.<br /><br />Wedding season is synonymous for “summer people” on Nantucket, and that is when the island is uncomfortably crammed full of people. When police chief Kapenash gets a call early one morning due to a body discovery in the water, the police quickly find out it is the maid of honor in a wedding that is to be held that day. It is safe to say, there would be no wedding.<br /><br />The book encompasses the investigation as to whom is responsible for the murder, and I was surprised by the ending. Because it’s a lighter mystery, I did not have to focus on analysis and detailed reading, and instead, I could relax and be completely entertained in this indulgent read from the first page to the last. <br /><br />I continue to be impressed with Hilderband’s ability to stay on top of her game. The Perfect Couple is a smart, inventive, dazzling, and successful work of light mystery dressed in beach read finery. <br /><br />Thank you to Little, Brown and Company and Netgalley for the copy. The Perfect Couple is now available! <br /><br />My reviews can also be found on my blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jennifertarheelreader.com">www.jennifertarheelreader.com</a> </span>

<div id="review_2583639297" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Cristina Monica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica"><img alt="Cristina Monica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589617514p2/14596170.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2583639297?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cristina Monica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristina Monica" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica">Cristina Monica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2583639297" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10518291933132263608">There are no such things as perfect couples… perfect relationships… perfect beings.<br/><br/>I was intimidated by this book. It has over 450 pages and the adult mysteries that I read in the past were all rather slow if no large amount of suspense was included.<br/><br/>But this mystery pulled me in from the very first page. It’s a fast-paced and addictive story. It’s not even that I became attached to the characters or found them particularly original, but the author had a lot to say.<br/><br/>And it felt as though she herse</span>
  <span id="freeText10518291933132263608" style="display:none">There are no such things as perfect couples… perfect relationships… perfect beings.<br /><br />I was intimidated by this book. It has over 450 pages and the adult mysteries that I read in the past were all rather slow if no large amount of suspense was included.<br /><br />But this mystery pulled me in from the very first page. It’s a fast-paced and addictive story. It’s not even that I became attached to the characters or found them particularly original, but the author had a lot to say.<br /><br />And it felt as though she herself was trying to figure out what happened to the dead maid. Who killed her? So many suspects… So many secrets… Drama, drama, drama.<br /><br />You know what I’ve learned recently? I’ve always kind of known that I respond to intensity, but I didn’t realize how much I love drama until I spend a whole day with someone who hates anything dramatic. I. Could. Not. Connect.<br /><br />So if, like me, you respond to drama and fast-paced stories, this is the right book for you! It may contain over 450 pages, but I read it in two days, three sittings, and honestly I wouldn’t have minded if it had been a little longer for more back-story on the characters. <br /><br />There are clichés that you will be able to spot right away, but that’s part of why it’s so darn dramatic and entertaining. And, by the way, there IS romance but this is a MYSTERY first and foremost. <br /><br /><a href="https://hitormissbooks.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/c/LolaReviewer" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a>Twitter</a> | <a>Instagram</a> | <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/105021852309973899120/posts" rel="nofollow noopener">Google+</a> | <a href="https://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/hit-miss-books-12564715" rel="nofollow noopener">Bloglovin’</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10518291933132263608" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2469980933" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2469980933" />
    <a title="Amanda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20971541-amanda"><img alt="Amanda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1377035138p2/20971541.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2469980933?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda" href="/user/show/20971541-amanda">Amanda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20971541-amanda?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2469980933" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17440400983469369496">I didn’t like this book I adored it. Whilst reading this amazing story was all I could think about, every time I HAD to put this book down, I likened it to having to put a film on hold and all the characters were paused, eager for my return so they could continue their story!!<br/><br/>The fairytale wedding between very wealthy Benji and Celeste should be the wedding of the year, no expense spared and all organised by the grooms Mother Greer.<br/><br/>On the morning of the wedding Maid of Honour Merritt is discover</span>
  <span id="freeText17440400983469369496" style="display:none">I didn’t like this book I adored it. Whilst reading this amazing story was all I could think about, every time I HAD to put this book down, I likened it to having to put a film on hold and all the characters were paused, eager for my return so they could continue their story!!<br /><br />The fairytale wedding between very wealthy Benji and Celeste should be the wedding of the year, no expense spared and all organised by the grooms Mother Greer.<br /><br />On the morning of the wedding Maid of Honour Merritt is discovered dead, that is when you realise all is not well in paradise and that there are many secrets to be revealed, before we find out what really happened to Merritt.<br /><br />What was there not to like in this book? It has everything I love in a novel, glamour, secrets, affairs and murder all nicely told in 2 timelines. The time leading up to Benji and Celeste meeting and falling in love and the lead up to their wedding. the characters are so wealthy and have amazing names like Merritt and Greer!! I looked up Nantucket and I’m desperate to go there now and have a tiny taste of paradise. <br /><br />I have to say even right at the end of the book, I hadn’t completely worked out what had happened to Merritt as everybody seemed to be hiding secrets and acting guiltily.<br /><br />I would love to read another book set in Nantucket with the same great characters appearing in it, especially Chief Ed Kapenash and Nick Diamantopoulos and what happens to all the other memorable characters!!<br /><br />This to my surprise is Elin Hildrebran’s twenty first novel and my first ever book I’ve read of hers, so I have some major catching up to do. I recommend you to read this book which should come with a warning that its highly addictive and you won’t be able to put it down!!<br /><br />After all that talk about Lobster I feel a craving coming on for some, and as the saying goes “If you can’t beat them join them”<br /><br />Thank you to Netgalley for my copy in exchange for a review. <br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17440400983469369496" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText6958877273734347570" style="display:none">The Queen of the "Beach Read" is holding onto that crown for one more year!!!!!<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34840184.The_Perfect_Couple" title="The Perfect Couple by Elin Hilderbrand" rel="nofollow noopener">The Perfect Couple</a> has something I always love from an <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/88301.Elin_Hilderbrand" title="Elin Hilderbrand" rel="nofollow noopener">Elin Hilderbrand</a> book - nods to characters from her old books. You need this book!!<br /><br />Thank you to Little Brown for an advanced copy. All opinions are my own.</span>

<div id="review_2489491517" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2489491517" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1394406877p2/2473504.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2489491517?book_show_action=true">Aug 10, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=womens-fiction-chicklit">womens-fiction-chicklit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=read-2018">read-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=listened-to-audiobook">listened-to-audiobook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2489491517" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4507568788044698018">I've read very little from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/88301.Elin_Hilderbrand' title='Elin Hilderbrand' rel='nofollow noopener'>Elin Hilderbrand</a>, but the ratings have been so high with this 2018 release that I just couldn't resist. I have to agree with the masses. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34840184.The_Perfect_Couple' title='The Perfect Couple by Elin Hilderbrand' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Perfect Couple</a> was a great read. It is an exploration of families and relationships with a death investigation as the backdrop. Key word: backdrop. In my opinion, if you view this story as only a murder mystery, you may leave severely disappointed. But if you open yourself up to meet a variety of characters with wide ranges of his</span>
  <span id="freeText4507568788044698018" style="display:none">I've read very little from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/88301.Elin_Hilderbrand" title="Elin Hilderbrand" rel="nofollow noopener">Elin Hilderbrand</a>, but the ratings have been so high with this 2018 release that I just couldn't resist. I have to agree with the masses. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34840184.The_Perfect_Couple" title="The Perfect Couple by Elin Hilderbrand" rel="nofollow noopener">The Perfect Couple</a> was a great read. It is an exploration of families and relationships with a death investigation as the backdrop. Key word: backdrop. In my opinion, if you view this story as only a murder mystery, you may leave severely disappointed. But if you open yourself up to meet a variety of characters with wide ranges of histories, dysfunction and values, then you might end up really enjoying the reading experience. Filled with drama, romance, mystery, secrets, complicated emotions and... did I say drama? Yep. Weddings will do that to you. But Hilderbrand also adds tenderness, love and support and I could not get enough. Fast-paced and entertaining, I thoroughly enjoyed <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34840184.The_Perfect_Couple" title="The Perfect Couple by Elin Hilderbrand" rel="nofollow noopener">The Perfect Couple</a>. I left the experience incredibly satisfied and very eager to check out more of Hilderbrand's books.<br /><br /><b>My favorite quote:</b><br /><i>"...nothing on this earth – and I mean nothing – prepares you for how much you love your kids. Am I right?"</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="4507568788044698018" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1126485836372284914">3.5 whodunit stars<br/><br/>Ah to be rich, gorgeous, and have the perfect summer retreat! Can anything be better, the beach, the sand, the sun, the boats, the mansion, the murder...what wait....Welcome to the summer world in Erin Hilderbrand's The Perfect Couple.<br/><br/> Everything is perfect on the island of Nantucket. It is the wedding weekend for Benji and Celeste, soon to be the perfect couple are to be wed.   <span id="freeText1126485836372284914" style="display:none">3.5 whodunit stars<br /><br />Ah to be rich, gorgeous, and have the perfect summer retreat! Can anything be better, the beach, the sand, the sun, the boats, the mansion, the murder...what wait....Welcome to the summer world in Erin Hilderbrand's The Perfect Couple.<br /><br /> Everything is perfect on the island of Nantucket. It is the wedding weekend for Benji and Celeste, soon to be the perfect couple are to be wed. The wedding thrown so lavishly and brilliantly by Benji's parents Tag and Greer Winbury, truly the perfect couple, will be a gala affair. All is ready, all is perfect and then the maid of honor is found dead floating in the water by the bride to be and perfection turns to mayhem as there is the possibility that she has been murdered. So much for perfection!<br /><br /> There are secrets circling and all that perfection does take on a huge hue of tarnishing. As the secrets unfold we find a family in an emotional chaos and the fun begins as the chief of police tries to find out what really happened to our maid of honor<br /><br />This was a quick easy read, one that was fraught with clues to the demise of said maid of honor. All the main participants had emotional whatnots going on and we find that perfection is not something any of them really carry around. I enjoyed the play of characters and the way in which this author unfurled their many indiscretions and foibles. The was my first book by Ms Hilderbrand's and I have to say I will be back for more "romantic" fun<br /><br />Thanks and a big shout out to my local library who every week provides our community with the new and fabulous in its patrons' reading pleasure.</span>

<div id="review_2399088808" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2399088808" />
    <a title="Zoe" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18237582-zoe"><img alt="Zoe" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460088540p2/18237582.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2399088808?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zoe" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zoe" href="/user/show/18237582-zoe">Zoe</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2399088808" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer570627139587573133">Compelling, mysterious, and deliciously entertaining!<br/><br/>The Perfect Couple takes us to the beautiful island of Nantucket and into the lives of the rich and famous Winburys as they gather to celebrate a family wedding. But like most families with privilege, power, and money everything is not always as it seems and it quickly becomes apparent that behind the beautiful mansion and designer clothes is an abundance of secrets, deception, betrayal, infidelity, substance abuse, lies, scandals, and murder.</span>
  <span id="freeText570627139587573133" style="display:none">Compelling, mysterious, and deliciously entertaining!<br /><br />The Perfect Couple takes us to the beautiful island of Nantucket and into the lives of the rich and famous Winburys as they gather to celebrate a family wedding. But like most families with privilege, power, and money everything is not always as it seems and it quickly becomes apparent that behind the beautiful mansion and designer clothes is an abundance of secrets, deception, betrayal, infidelity, substance abuse, lies, scandals, and murder.<br /><br />The writing is effortless and fluid. The characterization is spot on with a cast of characters that are flawed, authentic, and fun. And the alluring plot is an intelligent, lighthearted mix of a breezy summer read, unpredictable whodunit, and domestic drama all rolled up in one.<br /><br />Overall, The Perfect Couple is an enjoyable, scintillating treat by Hilderbrand that once again highlights her incredible ability to delve into all the complex dynamics between family members and friends and is without a doubt a must read for 2018!<br /><br />Thank you to Little, Brown and Company for providing me with a copy in exchange for an honest review.<br /><br />All my reviews can be found on my blog at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://whatsbetterthanbooks.com">https://whatsbetterthanbooks.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="570627139587573133" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2544212546" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544212546" />
    <a title="Margitte" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7481492-margitte"><img alt="Margitte" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1361772481p2/7481492.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2544212546?book_show_action=true">Sep 27, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Margitte" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Margitte" href="/user/show/7481492-margitte">Margitte</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/39293747-the-perfect-couple">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7481492-margitte?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7481492-margitte?shelf=american-author">american-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7481492-margitte?shelf=relationships">relationships</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7481492-margitte?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7481492-margitte?shelf=family-sagas">family-sagas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7481492-margitte?shelf=2018-releases">2018-releases</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7481492-margitte?shelf=women-s-fiction">women-s-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7481492-margitte?shelf=american-novel">american-novel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7481492-margitte?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7481492-margitte?shelf=drama">drama</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2544212546" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1171400204623422843">The last time a wedding had this kind of effect on me, was with <i>Did You Ever Have A Family</i> by Bill Clegg. ( my review just in case you're interested: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1820491063'>https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a>)<br/><br/>It was just a pleasant gathering of family and friends, and, well, you know the drill, a few shady characters who had to be invited. The wedding promised to be the epitome of class since Greer Garrison Winbury, an established snob with her British bloodline on full display, was at the helm to make this Nuntu</span>
  <span id="freeText1171400204623422843" style="display:none">The last time a wedding had this kind of effect on me, was with <i>Did You Ever Have A Family</i> by Bill Clegg. ( my review just in case you're interested: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1820491063">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a>)<br /><br />It was just a pleasant gathering of family and friends, and, well, you know the drill, a few shady characters who had to be invited. The wedding promised to be the epitome of class since Greer Garrison Winbury, an established snob with her British bloodline on full display, was at the helm to make this Nuntucket event worthy of the island's affluent residents. She thrived on tradition, protocol and decorum. Name is everything. And isn't Nantucket Island tasteful, charming, nautical, classic? Her husband Tag, gave her everything she ever wanted, except one thing; his devotion. It was actually him calling her a snob, a terrific snob, actually, but nonetheless deemed her worthy to be his wife for life, and celebrated her as the mother of their two children, Benji and Thomas. The wedding was meticulously planned for Benji and his quiet, stuttering bride, Celeste. Merrit Monaco was Celeste's best friend.<br /><br />Where is a better place to fish out scandals and secrets, than at a wedding? To be there and share in the joy, is a thrill. To be invited, make sure you promise a lucrative gift. Or give in to a bribe. Money talks. I'm just being coy here, don't mind me. Londonder Featherleigh Dale was one of those old family friends who invited herself and nobody could stop her... <br /><br />However, The Fourth of July, promised to go seriously sideways this year, when the bridesmaid, Merrit Monaco, was found dead on the eve of the wedding. Chief Ed Kapenash of the Nantucket Police Department was called out on Saturday, July 7, 2018, 5.53 am.<br /><br />And there goes the carefully manicured facades and facial perfections. Some were hysterical, others dark and brooding, as can be expected, right? Pacifiers were there in abundance: Mount Gay Black Barel rum was one, and the beers, and the champagne, and the cigars, and...and...simply water...<br /><br />But in the end....well...accidents sometimes acquire totally new meanings. This was one of those moments. <br /><br />I loved the ending, although many other readers were angry. They wanted the book to be something totally different, addressing their own prejudices. They were angry with the author for taking control of the plot back! She was controlling it anyway and left the reader with an unexpected possibility. Yep, my kind of ending.<br /><br />If I have a gripe with this book, it is the middle section where chick-lit reigned. Really, so uncalled for, unless it was the target audience in the first place. Well, let it be known in the blurb. But it is described as a beach read, and in that sense it is a perfect, fast-flowing,super one. Light, but intriguing, glitzy but grounded, a whodunnit with Veuve Cliquot bubbles lightening up the other side of tragedy.<br /><br />The two books, this one and <i>Did You Ever Have A Family</i> by Bill Clegg, had a wedding as center stage, with the same mystery and magic of family and friends becoming unraveled and a tragic event exposing the under garments which support the perfect image. When those hidden layers start dropping, the perfection reacts like a face lift going haywire when the lights come on. The difference between the two novels is the intended audiences. <i>The Perfect Couple</i> intended to entertain. Bill Clegg's book had a much deeper dimension. It was though-provoking, emotionally challenging, and really riveting.<br /><br />Nevertheless, I wanted to read something lighter and <i>The Perfect Couple</i> was a good choice. The ending will make you think. It is unexpected, sad, but surprising. I loved that. But it is undoubtedly a slightly raunchy chick-lit experience with a whodunit thrown in to expand the possible reading audience.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1171400204623422843" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6120245577906936909">Okay, where to begin.. I LOVED THIS BOOK. This is one where I had to put it down to stop myself from reading it in one sitting because I wanted it to last. This is also one that I accidentally left out in a storm and ruined it, so I immediately ordered a new one on Amazon because I had to finish it and I had to have copy myself because I know I'm going to be lending this one to friends.<br/><br/>The Perfect Couple follows a bunch of people attending a high-end Nantucket weddings. Everything seems perfect </span>
  <span id="freeText6120245577906936909" style="display:none">Okay, where to begin.. I LOVED THIS BOOK. This is one where I had to put it down to stop myself from reading it in one sitting because I wanted it to last. This is also one that I accidentally left out in a storm and ruined it, so I immediately ordered a new one on Amazon because I had to finish it and I had to have copy myself because I know I'm going to be lending this one to friends.<br /><br />The Perfect Couple follows a bunch of people attending a high-end Nantucket weddings. Everything seems perfect until the maid of honor ends up dead. Is it suicide or murder? The detectives have to get everyones story and as you can imagine, nothing is as it seems. <br /><br />I've read a lot of murder mystery/suspense books lately but I haven't fallen into one quite like I did with The Perfect Couple. The characters are all so weirdly likable in their own ways. They are brilliantly written and the author does a wonderful job of going back and forth both in time and characters. It is a bit longer which is great because you really get the feel for who everyone is and the interpersonal relations. <br /><br />I didn't know who to root for in this one. Even the worst characters had their redeeming moments and the lovable ones some questionable moments. I can't recommend this book enough. <br /><br />My only concern and why I'm going back and forth between giving this 4 1/2 stars or 5 (I'm settling on 4 1/2 but rounding up for Goodreads) is the ending. It was so not what I was expecting. At first I was definitely disappointed but the more I think about it I can see that it works. I wish there was more closure for these characters that I loved but really this was one of my favorite reads all summer. <br /><br />Are all of Elin Hilderbrand's books this good? Because if they are I think I just found one of my new favorite authors!</span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36306720-the-perfect-couple">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57073687-nadia?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57073687-nadia?shelf=best-of-2018">best-of-2018</a>,

<span id="freeTextContainer6976513553350311136">I surprised myself how much I enjoyed this book. I was staying away from Hilderbrand thinking her books were female fiction, full of romance, which is rarely my thing. And so I was very hesitant to pick this up. However, after reading some great reviews from my GR friends I decided to give it a go. And I'm sooo glad I did. <br/><br/><br/>First of all, I want to point out that the Perfect Couple is a murder mystery! Perhaps that contributed to how much I adored it?  The book starts on the morning of Celeste's w</span>
  <span id="freeText6976513553350311136" style="display:none">I surprised myself how much I enjoyed this book. I was staying away from Hilderbrand thinking her books were female fiction, full of romance, which is rarely my thing. And so I was very hesitant to pick this up. However, after reading some great reviews from my GR friends I decided to give it a go. And I'm sooo glad I did. <br /><br /><br />First of all, I want to point out that the Perfect Couple is a murder mystery! Perhaps that contributed to how much I adored it?  The book starts on the morning of Celeste's wedding day, when a dead body of her maid of honour is found on the shore of Nantucket. The timeline then jumps from the present to the past revealing the relationships between the wedding guests and their history. There are at least a couple of chapters focusing on each main character which I thoroughly enjoyed. Hilderbrand managed to portray everyone in such a vivid way that they all seemed very alive to me. I found the realistic aspect of the novel even more profound by incorporating the little details such as the titles of the books the characters were reading, places they visited in Europe - all very familiar to me.<br /><br /><br />The novel is based on the island of Nantucket. I haven't been to Nantucket but got engaged next door at Martha's Vineyard last year so felt a bit of connection to the atmosphere and vibe of the place.<br /><br /><br />This was my first Hilderbrand novel and it gets 5 stars for me. I do realise however that I might have lucked out by picking this one as my first book and might not like her other books as much. Who knows.. I will have to read another one and see for myself.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_2168742436" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2168742436" />
    <a title="Amy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14045562-amy"><img alt="Amy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1542231656p2/14045562.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2168742436?book_show_action=true">May 24, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy" href="/user/show/14045562-amy">Amy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14045562-amy?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14045562-amy?shelf=best-womens-fiction-2018">best-womens-fiction-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14045562-amy?shelf=best-of-2018">best-of-2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2168742436" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9452572124557568087">I’ve said it before and I’m sure I’ll repeat myself every single summer, but summer doesn’t officially start for me until I’ve read the latest Elin Hilderbrand novel. While I have several authors on my summer must read list every year, hers are the books I look forward to the most, she really is the queen of the beach read and The Perfect Couple is her best book yet!<br/><br/>While Hilderbrand’s books definitely aren’t always sunshine and cocktails, this was a bit of a departure from her previous books. T</span>
  <span id="freeText9452572124557568087" style="display:none">I’ve said it before and I’m sure I’ll repeat myself every single summer, but summer doesn’t officially start for me until I’ve read the latest Elin Hilderbrand novel. While I have several authors on my summer must read list every year, hers are the books I look forward to the most, she really is the queen of the beach read and The Perfect Couple is her best book yet!<br /><br />While Hilderbrand’s books definitely aren’t always sunshine and cocktails, this was a bit of a departure from her previous books. There’s still that wonderful ensemble cast where you feel like you’re a fly on the wall, and there’s also the stunning backdrop of the now familiar beaches of Nantucket, but this had a slightly darker feel since there’s a murder mystery at its core. Think Liane Moriarty in terms of vibe but set it among the super elite and wealthy and that’s TPC.<br /><br />This was yet another effortless read, super entertaining and a true page turner. Hilderbrand is such a great writer, she really brings Nantucket to life, you can smell the lobster rolls, feel the sand between your toes and imagine you’re surrounded by the glitzy characters who reside in Nantucket. These characters all had juicy secrets and problems and I was eager to find out what really happened to Merritt and along the way there were plenty of turns. A few characters from her previous novels are featured, catching up on their lives was awesome, especially Chief Ed as The Castaways was one of my favorite books. Recommended to everyone, I’m calling it the must read book of the summer purely based on it’s fun factor alone but it’s incredibly well written and plotted to perfection boot, the ultimate summer read.<br /><br />The Perfect Couple in three words: Juicy, Secretive and Fun.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9452572124557568087" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2758514032?book_show_action=true">Mar 22, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cortney LaScola - The Bookworm Myrtle Beach" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cortney LaScola - The Bookworm Myrtle Beach" href="/user/show/6320671-cortney-lascola---the-bookworm-myrtle-beach">Cortney LaScola - The Bookworm Myrtle Beach</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780316375269" href="/book/show/36341607-the-perfect-couple">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2758514032" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1392219750816563154">3.5 stars rounded down<br/><br/>This was my first Elin Hilderbrand... it was good, but I was not amazed. I don't know if it's because I usually read mystery/suspense books, and this was her first attempt at that type of book? It was a good story, but nothing but Merritt's death was resolved in the end. What happened to all the characters? Basically everyone's life was in shambles, and we have no answers or conclusions.<br/><br/>The author's rambling on and on about this clothing designer, this antique, this fancy f</span>
  <span id="freeText1392219750816563154" style="display:none">3.5 stars rounded down<br /><br />This was my first Elin Hilderbrand... it was good, but I was not amazed. I don't know if it's because I usually read mystery/suspense books, and this was her first attempt at that type of book? It was a good story, but nothing but Merritt's death was resolved in the end. What happened to all the characters? Basically everyone's life was in shambles, and we have no answers or conclusions.<br /><br />The author's rambling on and on about this clothing designer, this antique, this fancy food in such detail got kind of annoying. They're rich, we get it. Cutting out all that unnecessary stuff would have hacked a good chunk of pages out this almost 500 page book. Also, calling the one cop "The Greek" really rubbed me the wrong way. Like, what?? This is 2019, right?<br /><br />I think I would have been better off starting with one of her usual beachy reads instead of The Perfect Couple. I'm sure I'll pick another one of her books up in the future, but I don't feel a burning need to do it right away.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1392219750816563154" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2873001838" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2873001838" />
    <a title="Monica (crazy_4_books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/97023221-monica-crazy-4-books"><img alt="Monica (crazy_4_books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606106899p2/97023221.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2873001838?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Monica (crazy_4_books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Monica (crazy_4_books)" href="/user/show/97023221-monica-crazy-4-books">Monica (crazy_4_books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781473611269" href="/book/show/40213174-the-perfect-couple">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/97023221-monica-crazy-4-books?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/97023221-monica-crazy-4-books?shelf=reviews">reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/97023221-monica-crazy-4-books?shelf=greatest-hits">greatest-hits</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2873001838" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1700992519174723284">“SECRETS & LIES IN NANTUCKET TOWN”<br/>(#2 book read for the buzzword readathon hosted by Booksandlala)<br/>This book was surprisingly cool! It has such Liane Moriarty’s “Big Little Lies” vibes. I know this is Elin Hilderbrand’s first murder mystery novel, and the first of her many books I’ve read, but I’m quite intrigued to pick up other backlist tiles and will definitely buy “Summer of ‘69”. I had this one on my bookcase for months, now I regret not picking up sooner. I did not think I was going to like</span>
  <span id="freeText1700992519174723284" style="display:none">“SECRETS &amp; LIES IN NANTUCKET TOWN”<br />(#2 book read for the buzzword readathon hosted by Booksandlala)<br />This book was surprisingly cool! It has such Liane Moriarty’s “Big Little Lies” vibes. I know this is Elin Hilderbrand’s first murder mystery novel, and the first of her many books I’ve read, but I’m quite intrigued to pick up other backlist tiles and will definitely buy “Summer of ‘69”. I had this one on my bookcase for months, now I regret not picking up sooner. I did not think I was going to like it as much as I did. It is perfect for those who like cozy mystery books, without violence or bloody scenes. That is why it reminded me of “Big Little Lies”: there is a murder, an investigation conducted by the local chief of police in present day and flashbacks to the day before and some flashbacks that go back months or years before the event. It never got confusing or boring, I kept reading despite being tired because I was actually puzzled, and I have to admit I had lot of theories of who the killer or killers could be, but did not see that ending coming.<br />Big wedding coming up on a Saturday in July, expensive one, like the one in that movie with Robert De Niro and Diane Keaton. Early in the morning of the wedding, the bride wakes everyone up screaming like a mad woman because she has found the dead body of her best friend, AKA the maid of honor, drowned by the shore. It looks like an accidental death but the police and we (the readers) know better. An investigation starts that expands all Saturday. That is the present timeline. We also learn everything that happened the day before, Friday, the dead woman’s last day on Earth, told by POVs of different characters. There are many characters and some of them have a motive for killing the victim. Everyone has something to hide; only the groom is kind of a dummy. The list of suspects is long: the bride, the groom, the best man, the groom’s father (the asshole), the groom’s mother (rich bitch), the bride’s parents (her mother is dying of cancer, not a spoiler), the groom’s brother and sister-in-law, and some British cougar that crashed the party to get revenge on one of the guests. <br />So far, I have not spoiled anything. We realize that everyone has secrets and some of them huge motives to get the victim out of the way. I found myself having to reach the ending without knowing for sure who did it. In conclusion, the book is catchy, fast-paced, enjoyable and quite appealing. Glad I picked it up for the readathon.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1700992519174723284" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2396564819" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2396564819" />
    <a title="NZLisaM" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/79324789-nzlisam"><img alt="NZLisaM" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521069706p2/79324789.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2396564819?book_show_action=true">Jun 21, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NZLisaM" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NZLisaM" href="/user/show/79324789-nzlisam">NZLisaM</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79324789-nzlisam?shelf=crime">crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79324789-nzlisam?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79324789-nzlisam?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79324789-nzlisam?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79324789-nzlisam?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/79324789-nzlisam?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2396564819" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16343792623119708454">Oh, what a tangled web we weave, or crikey, this wedding party sure had a lot to hide!<br/><br/>Upon reading the book blurb for this one, I knew I just had to pre-order it – a beautiful island wedding where the guests are all staying at the same location, and the maid of honour is found dead – sold! And did it live up to my expectations – yes, yes, yes! I knew going in that it was going to be tamer than my usual crime read, leaning more towards contemporary drama, which it was, but I have to say it was a </span>
  <span id="freeText16343792623119708454" style="display:none">Oh, what a tangled web we weave, or crikey, this wedding party sure had a lot to hide!<br /><br />Upon reading the book blurb for this one, I knew I just had to pre-order it – a beautiful island wedding where the guests are all staying at the same location, and the maid of honour is found dead – sold! And did it live up to my expectations – yes, yes, yes! I knew going in that it was going to be tamer than my usual crime read, leaning more towards contemporary drama, which it was, but I have to say it was a nice change of pace for me, and I really enjoyed it. The mystery plot, which I worried might be too obvious, wasn’t, and even when I thought I had worked it out, turns out I was wrong. <br /><br />There’s a lot of glamour and glitz, talk of décor, scenery, parties, outings, heaps of descriptions of food and drink (which all sounded delicious by the way) but again that was a given before I even opened the book, and was told in such an interesting, insightful way, that I even relished those parts. Nantucket Island sure does sound like a gorgeous place, and the author definitely did it justice. <br /><br />The story opens with the Chief of Police receiving a phone call that the maid of honour has been found floating in the ocean, on the morning of the wedding day, and covers the subsequent investigation that follows. There are also multiple flashbacks to the day before the wedding, as well as the two years leading up to the event. At times the story is pretty heartbreaking and tragic, so keep those tissues handy, but there’s also some amusing and touching moments that have you smiling. <br /><br />After perusing Elin Hilderbrand’s other books, it looks like this is the authors first mystery novel, and I’m keeping my fingers crossed she writes more in this vein, as she did an amazing job. Even though it’s winter here, and I read under the covers with the electric blanket, this would make an excellent summer beach read, as it’s easy to read, and follow.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16343792623119708454" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2490722575" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7095179460679859665">4 Summery Stars to "The Perfect Couple"<br/><br/>I've been waiting all summer to get my hands on this book and I was able to read right before back-to-school! This book cements for me that I must get to Nantucket soon. I loved the descriptions of the beach house and island and Hilderbrand does such a great job populating her books with interesting characters!<br/><br/>This one has a meatier plot than some of Hilderbrand's other books that I've read. This one still has lots of relationship development, but a dead we</span>
  <span id="freeText7095179460679859665" style="display:none">4 Summery Stars to "The Perfect Couple"<br /><br />I've been waiting all summer to get my hands on this book and I was able to read right before back-to-school! This book cements for me that I must get to Nantucket soon. I loved the descriptions of the beach house and island and Hilderbrand does such a great job populating her books with interesting characters!<br /><br />This one has a meatier plot than some of Hilderbrand's other books that I've read. This one still has lots of relationship development, but a dead wedding guest complicates things. There are police interviews, secrets uncovered, and a whodunit element. Now that I think about it, I'm wondering who the title refers to? Maybe from the outside there are some perfect couples, but by the book's end, much is unraveled! <br /><br />If you've enjoyed Hilderbrand's other books, I'm pretty sure you'll like this one too. I'm curious to see if this is a new genre for this writer or if she'll go back to relationship-only driven books.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7095179460679859665" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9254240961144290031">HORRIBLE. I would have given this 0 stars if I could. I think I am officially done with Elin. I have read all of her books and very much looked forward to any new book she put out. Maybe she needs to take the advice she smugly gives to the author in this book and retire. The past few stories have been meh, at best. This was painful. It didn't help that I listened to the audio book and the narrator was terrible, several mispronunciations. The story line was predictable, the characters were unlika</span>
  <span id="freeText9254240961144290031" style="display:none">HORRIBLE. I would have given this 0 stars if I could. I think I am officially done with Elin. I have read all of her books and very much looked forward to any new book she put out. Maybe she needs to take the advice she smugly gives to the author in this book and retire. The past few stories have been meh, at best. This was painful. It didn't help that I listened to the audio book and the narrator was terrible, several mispronunciations. The story line was predictable, the characters were unlikable and even the Nantucket background that she, in the past, has painted so lovely was dull. </span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_36344555'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/36344555-all-we-ever-wanted"><img alt="All We Ever Wanted" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1512578976l/36344555._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/ZNLdqoyGacgmq1jeyxamDDhu0DJNd3uUnKKXY1PaRjoA9roE+HQXxFURi2do0AsSfhEHMovNif/MjIgfNfprg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/88301.Elin_Hilderbrand">About Elin Hilderbrand</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer7757765108625384002">Elin Hilderbrand lives on Nantucket with her husband and their three young children. She grew up in Collegeville, Pennsylvania, and traveled extensively before settling on Nantucket, which has been the setting for her five previous novels. Hilderbrand is a graduate of Johns Hopkins University and the graduate fiction workshop at the University of Iowa.<br/><br/><a href='http://www.facebook.com/ElinHilderbrand' rel='nofollow noopener'>Facebook.com/ElinHilderbrand</a><br/><br/><a href='http://pinterest.com/elinhilderbrand/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pinterest.com/Elin</a></span>
  <span id="freeText7757765108625384002" style="display:none">Elin Hilderbrand lives on Nantucket with her husband and their three young children. She grew up in Collegeville, Pennsylvania, and traveled extensively before settling on Nantucket, which has been the setting for her five previous novels. Hilderbrand is a graduate of Johns Hopkins University and the graduate fiction workshop at the University of Iowa.<br /><br /><a href="http://www.facebook.com/ElinHilderbrand" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook.com/ElinHilderbrand</a><br /><br /><a href="http://pinterest.com/elinhilderbrand/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest.com/ElinHilderbrand</a></span>
